Our client provides solutions in multiple segments including Retail Banking Products, Business Products, Investment Products, and International Remittance services. The retail Banking segment includes services and products for individuals, including deposits, financing, remittances, and currency exchange. The Corporate Banking segment comprises services and products to corporate and commercial customers, including deposits, financing, and trade services. The Treasury segment offers money market, trading, and treasury services. The Investment Banking and Brokerage segment consists of investment management services and asset management activities related to dealing, managing, arranging, advising, and custody of securities.

About the role:
As a
Senior Business Analyst
, become a part of a cross-functional development team working for our Client.
About the Client:
Client enterprise application access product provides enterprise end-users access to enterprise owned services provisioned in some enterprise data centers. Users are first authenticated by an enterprise preferred identity provider and access is restricted to only those services that the authenticated user is authorized to access.
Many critical enterprise client-server applications, require the ability to transport arbitrary TCP/UDP based protocols traffic between a native mobile app on the user
‚Äô
s device and the application server in the customer's datacenter. To support these use cases, product will support iOS, Android and ChromeOS client applications.
Responsibilities:

Interact with product manager on product strategy definition and target market segments
Evaluate business analysis processes and continuously improve them. Establish and follow requirements lifecycle processes
Mentor other analysts on request. Organize knowledge sharing and training sessions for other analysts. Contribute to the corporate knowledge base
Monitor solution implementation and conduct internal and external solution acceptance. Manage solution acceptance criteria
Care about continuous improvement of customer satisfaction

‚Äî –í–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—è –æ–ø–∏—Å—É–≤–∞—Ç–∏ —Å–∫–ª–∞–¥–Ω—ñ —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω—ñ—á–Ω—ñ —Ç–∞ –±—ñ–∑–Ω–µ—Å –∫–æ–Ω—Ü–µ–ø—Ü—ñ—ó –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ—é —Ç–∞ –∑—Ä–æ–∑—É–º—ñ–ª–æ—é –º–æ–≤–æ—é, –≤–µ—Å—Ç–∏ —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω—ñ—á–Ω—É –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü—ñ—é
‚Äî –í–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—è –∞–Ω–∞–ª—ñ–∑—É–≤–∞—Ç–∏ –≤–µ–ª–∏–∫—ñ –æ–±—Å—è–≥–∏ —ñ–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü—ñ—ó, —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—É–≤–∞—Ç–∏ —Ç–∞ –≤–∏–¥—ñ–ª—è—Ç–∏ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–µ
‚Äî –†–æ–∑—É–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—è –∞—Ä—Ö—ñ—Ç–µ–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∏ —Ä–æ–∑—Ä–æ–±–∫–∏ —Ç–∞ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—Ü–∏–ø—ñ–≤ —ñ–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü—ñ—ó
‚Äî –°–∏–ª—å–Ω—ñ –∞–Ω–∞–ª—ñ—Ç–∏—á–Ω—ñ —Ç–∞ –∫–æ–º—É–Ω—ñ–∫–∞—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ñ –∑–¥—ñ–±–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—ñ
‚Äî –£–≤–∞–≥–∞ –¥–æ –¥–µ—Ç–∞–ª–µ–π, —Ñ–æ–∫—É—Å –Ω–∞ —è–∫—ñ—Å—Ç—å
‚Äî –í–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—è –±—Ä–∞—Ç–∏ –≤—ñ–¥–ø–æ–≤—ñ–¥–∞–ª—å–Ω—ñ—Å—Ç—å —Ç–∞ –ø—Ä–∏–π–º–∞—Ç–∏ —Ä—ñ—à–µ–Ω–Ω—è
–ë—É–¥–µ –ø–ª—é—Å–æ–º:
‚Äî –¥–æ—Å–≤—ñ–¥ —Ä–æ–±–æ—Ç–∏ –∑ Jira, Confluence, Postman

‚Äî –ø—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏—á–Ω–∏–π –¥–æ—Å–≤—ñ–¥ —Ä–æ–±–æ—Ç–∏ –≤ UML, BPMN, XML, JSON
‚Äî –¥–æ—Å–≤—ñ–¥ —Ä–æ–±–æ—Ç–∏ –∑ Swagger
‚Äî —Ä–æ–∑—É–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—è —Ä–æ–±–æ—Ç–∏ –≤ —Ç–µ–ª–µ–∫–æ–º –∫–æ–º–ø–∞–Ω—ñ—ó (–±—ñ–ª—ñ–Ω–≥ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∏, POP\PRP)
‚Äî –Ω–∞–≤–∏—á–∫–∏ —Ä–æ–±–æ—Ç–∏ –∑ API –±–µ–∫-–µ–Ω–¥ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º (—á–∏—Ç–∞–Ω–Ω—è —Ç–µ—Ö –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü—ñ—ó, —Ä–æ–∑—É–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—è —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∏ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç—É —Ç–∞ –≤—ñ–¥–ø–æ–≤—ñ–¥—ñ —É —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç—ñ JSON: API, SOAP)
–û–±–æ–≤‚Äô—è–∑–∫–∏:
‚Äî –ü–æ—à—É–∫ –º–∞–∫—Å–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ –æ–ø—Ç–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–≥–æ –≤–∞—Ä—ñ–∞–Ω—Ç–∞ –≤–∏—Ä—ñ—à–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–æ—ó –≤–∏–º–æ–≥–∏ —É —ñ—Å–Ω—É—é—á–æ–º—É –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª—ñ–∫—É —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º, –æ–ø—Ä–∞—Ü—é–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—è –±—ñ–∑–Ω–µ—Å —Å—Ü–µ–Ω–∞—Ä—ñ—ó–≤ —ñ–∑ –∑–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω—å
‚Äî –°—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—è, –¥–µ—Ç–∞–ª—ñ–∑–∞—Ü—ñ—è —Ç–∞ –ø—ñ–¥—Ç—Ä–∏–º–∫–∞ —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω—ñ—á–Ω–æ—ó –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü—ñ—ó (–¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü—ñ—è –ø–æ –ø—Ä–æ–¥—É–∫—Ç—É —Ç–∞ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å–∞–º: –±—ñ–∑–Ω–µ—Å –≤–∏–º–æ–≥–∏, –æ–ø–∏—Å–∏ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–Ω–∏—Ö –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç—ñ–≤ —Ç–∞ –∞—Ä—Ö—ñ—Ç–µ–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∏, web API-–¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∏, —Å–ø–µ—Ü–∏—Ñ—ñ–∫–∞—Ü—ñ—ó, user journey schemes)
‚Äî –ü—ñ–¥—Ç—Ä–∏–º–∫–∞ —Ç–∞ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–≥–ª—è–¥ —ñ—Å–Ω—É—é—á–æ—ó –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü—ñ—ó, –Ω–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–Ω—è —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω—ñ—á–Ω–æ—ó –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü—ñ—ó –∑ –Ω—É–ª—è –¥–ª—è –Ω–æ–≤–∏—Ö —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ–æ–Ω–∞–ª—ñ–≤
‚Äî –ó–±—ñ—Ä —ñ–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü—ñ—ó –ø—Ä–æ –æ–±–º–µ–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—è —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º —Ç–∞ –≤—ñ–¥–æ–±—Ä–∞–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—è —ó—Ö —É –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü—ñ—ó (–Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥, –º—ñ–Ω—ñ–º–∞–ª—å–Ω—ñ –≤–µ—Ä—Å—ñ—ó –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–∞, —â–æ –ø—ñ–¥—Ç—Ä–∏–º—É—é—Ç—å—Å—è, –º–∞–∫—Å–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω–∞ –∫—ñ–ª—å–∫—ñ—Å—Ç—å –æ–¥–Ω–æ—á–∞—Å–Ω–∏—Ö –∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–≤–∞—á—ñ–≤).
‚Äî –ü—ñ–¥–≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∫–∞ –≥—Ä–∞—Ñ—ñ—á–Ω–∏—Ö —Å—Ö–µ–º —Ç–∞ —Å—Ö–µ–º –±—ñ–∑–Ω–µ—Å-–ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—ñ–≤ –¥–ª—è —Ä–µ–∞–ª—ñ–∑–∞—Ü—ñ—ó –ø–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—Ö –∑–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω—å
‚Äî –û—Ü—ñ–Ω—é–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—è –æ–±—Å—è–≥—ñ–≤ –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü—ñ—ó —Ç–∞ —Ä–æ–∑—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø—Ä—ñ–æ—Ä–∏—Ç–µ—Ç—ñ–≤ –∑–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω—å –¥–ª—è –¥–æ—Ç—Ä–∏–º–∞–Ω–Ω—è —Ç–µ—Ä–º—ñ–Ω—ñ–≤
‚Äî –ö–æ–º—É–Ω—ñ–∫–∞—Ü—ñ—è –∑ —É—á–∞—Å–Ω–∏–∫–∞–º–∏ –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥–∏ (Product owner, developers, QA, UX/UI designer, –Ω–µ—Ç–µ—Ö–Ω—ñ—á–Ω—ñ —Å–ø–µ—Ü—ñ–∞–ª—ñ—Å—Ç–∏)

. –§–æ—Ä–º—É—î–º–æ —Ü–∏—Ñ—Ä–æ–≤—É —Ä–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω—ñ—Å—Ç—å, —Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ä—é—é—á–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–¥—É–∫—Ç–∏ –π —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω–æ–ª–æ–≥—ñ—ó –≤ –≥–∞–ª—É–∑—ñ social discovery —Ç–∞ –æ–Ω–ª–∞–π–Ω-–∑–Ω–∞–π–æ–º—Å—Ç–≤.

–ù–∞—à —Ñ–ª–∞–≥–º–∞–Ω—Å—å–∫–∏–π –ø—Ä–æ–¥—É–∫—Ç ‚Äî –º—ñ–∂–Ω–∞—Ä–æ–¥–Ω–∞ –ø–ª–∞—Ç—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞ –¥–ª—è –∑–Ω–∞–π–æ–º—Å—Ç–≤, —è–∫–∞ –¥–æ–ø–æ–º–∞–≥–∞—î —Å–ø—ñ–ª–∫—É–≤–∞—Ç–∏—Å—è –ª—é–¥—è–º –∑—ñ —Å–ø—ñ–ª—å–Ω–∏–º–∏ —Ü—ñ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—è–º–∏ —Ç–∞ —ñ–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–µ—Å–∞–º–∏ –ø–æ –≤—Å—å–æ–º—É —Å–≤—ñ—Ç—É. 9 —Ä–æ–∫—ñ–≤ —Ä–æ–±–æ—Ç–∏ –Ω–∞–¥ –ø—Ä–æ–¥—É–∫—Ç–æ–º, –±—ñ–ª—å—à –Ω—ñ–∂ 37 –º—ñ–ª—å–π–æ–Ω—ñ–≤ –∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–≤–∞—á—ñ–≤, —Ä–æ–∑–≤–∏—Ç–æ–∫ —É 20 –∫—Ä–∞—ó–Ω–∞—Ö, –∫–æ–º—É–Ω—ñ–∫–∞—Ü—ñ—è 8 –º–æ–≤–∞–º–∏, 3 –ø–ª–∞—Ç—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∏: WEB, Android —Ç–∞ iOS. –í—Å–µ —Ü–µ —Å—Ç–∞–ª–æ –º–æ–∂–ª–∏–≤–∏–º –∑–∞–≤–¥—è–∫–∏ –Ω–∞—à–∏–º —Å–ø—ñ–≤—Ä–æ–±—ñ—Ç–Ω–∏–∫–∞–º ‚Äî –∫–≤–∞—Ä–∫–∞–º.
–•—Ç–æ –Ω–∞—à —ñ–¥–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω–∏–π –∫–≤–∞—Ä–∫ –Ω–∞ —Ü—é –ø–æ—Å–∞–¥—É?
–ù–∞—à —ñ–¥–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω–∏–π –∫–∞–Ω–¥–∏–¥–∞—Ç ‚Äî –ª—é–¥–∏–Ω–∞, —è–∫–∞ –Ω–µ –±–æ—ó—Ç—å—Å—è –≤–µ–ª–∏–∫–∏—Ö –æ–±—Å—è–≥—ñ–≤ —Ä–æ–±–æ—Ç–∏, –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∞ –ø—Ä–∞—Ü—é–≤–∞—Ç–∏ –Ω–∞ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç, –≤–º—ñ—î —Å–∞–º–æ—Å—Ç—ñ–π–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–∏–π–º–∞—Ç–∏ —Ä—ñ—à–µ–Ω–Ω—è —Ç–∞ —Ö–æ—á–µ —Ä–æ–∑–≤–∏–≤–∞—Ç–∏—Å—è —É –Ω–∞–ø—Ä—è–º–∫—É –º–∞—Ä–∫–µ—Ç–∏–Ω–≥–æ–≤–æ—ó –∞–Ω–∞–ª—ñ—Ç–∏–∫–∏.
–Ø–∫–∏–º –±—É–¥–µ –ø–µ—Ä—à–∏–π —Ä–æ–±–æ—á–∏–π –¥–µ–Ω—å?
–û–Ω–±–æ—Ä–¥—ñ–Ω–≥ –º–∏–Ω–∞—Ç–∏–º–µ –Ω–µ–≤–∏–º—É—à–µ–Ω–æ: —Ç—ñ–º–ª—ñ–¥ –ø–æ–∑–Ω–∞–π–æ–º–∏—Ç—å —Ç–µ–±–µ –∑ –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥–æ—é, help desk –∑–∞–±–µ–∑–ø–µ—á–∏—Ç—å –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö—ñ–¥–Ω–æ—é —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω—ñ–∫–æ—é, –∞ –æ—Ñ—ñc-–º–µ–Ω–µ–¥–∂–µ—Ä –ø–æ–¥–∞—Ä—É—î welcome kit –≤—ñ–¥ –∫–æ–º–ø–∞–Ω—ñ—ó. –†–∞–Ω–∫–æ–≤–∞ –∫–∞–≤–∞, —Å–ø—ñ–ª–∫—É–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—è –∑ –∫–æ–ª–µ–≥–∞–º–∏, –∑–∞–Ω—É—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—è –≤ —ñ—Å—Ç–æ—Ä—ñ—é —Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—è –Ω–µ–π–º—ñ–Ω–≥—É —Ç–∞ —Å–º–∞—á–Ω–∏–π –æ–±—ñ–¥ ‚Äî –æ—Å—å, —â–æ —á–µ–∫–∞—Ç–∏–º–µ –Ω–∞ —Ç–µ–±–µ, —è–∫—â–æ —Ç–≤—ñ–π –≤–∏–±—ñ—Ä –ø—Ä–∞—Ü—é–≤–∞—Ç–∏ —Å–∞–º–µ –∑ –æ—Ñ—ñ—Å—É. –ñ–æ–¥–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Ö–≤–∏–ª—é–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—è —á–∏ –¥–µ–¥–ª–∞–π–Ω—ñ–≤, –ø–µ—Ä—à–∏–π —Ä–æ–±–æ—á–∏–π –¥–µ–Ω—å —É
Quarks
‚Äî –ª–∞–π—Ç–æ–≤–∏–π —ñ –ø—Ä–∏—î–º–Ω–∏–π.

. –ê–Ω–∞–ª—ñ—Ç–∏–∫, —è–∫–æ–≥–æ –º–∏ —à—É–∫–∞—î–º–æ ‚Äî —Ü–µ –Ω–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω–∞–≤–µ—Ü—å —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω—ñ—á–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∑–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è. –í–∞–∂–ª–∏–≤–æ –≤–∏—Å–ª–æ–≤–ª—é–≤–∞—Ç–∏ –¥—É–º–∫—É, –¥–æ–Ω–æ—Å–∏—Ç–∏ —ó—ó –¥–æ –∫–æ–ª–µ–≥ —Ç–∞ –ø—Ä–∏–π–º–∞—Ç–∏ –≤—ñ–¥–ø–æ–≤—ñ–¥–∞–ª—å–Ω—ñ —Ä—ñ—à–µ–Ω–Ω—è;

------------------------Reference Number: DQA1022
The Role:
We are looking for a passionate and experienced Data Quality Analyst to join our fast-growing team! The successful candidate will join the Data Governance team responsible for collaborating with our main IT stakeholders and the business data consumers to deliver data quality analysis and profiling of the company‚Äôs critical data to drive business improvement, embed data ownership and work closely with stakeholders to define data quality rules. In addition, the role will help lead the establishment of effective data quality monitoring, create visualisations through dashboards and support the resolution of data related issues.
The main responsibilities of the position include:
Implement data quality measurements on critical data
Perform statistical tests on large datasets to determine data quality and integrity
Gather data from primary or secondary data sources to identify and interpret trends
Perform root cause analysis to discover the cause of data issues
Collaborate with database developers to improve data collection and storage processes
Monitor, investigate, and correct data errors as needed
Support data improvement programmes and assist data stewards to rectify data issues
Report data analysis findings to management to inform business decisions and prioritise information system needs
Escalate urgent issues to team leader for help in resolution
Create dashboards and reports using visualisation tools
Produce data quality reports and scorecards for all key data assets
Main requirements:
BSc/MSc in statistics, mathematics, computer science, information management, any other related
Minimum 3 years‚Äô experience in a similar position
Hands-on experience in the manipulation, integration, processing, and interrogation of large datasets
Experience in issue management, remediation, and performance reporting/dashboards
In-depth knowledge of statistical methods and tests
Solid knowledge in programming languages, including Structured Query Language (SQL) and Python/R
Experience authoring, maintaining and executing data quality rules and reporting performance
Experienced in the application of data quality toolsets and business intelligence tooling
Exceptional analytical and problem-solving skills
Excellent interpersonal and communication skills
Benefit from:
Attractive remuneration package plus performance related reward
Food allowance
Intellectually stimulating work environment
Continuous personal development and international training opportunities
Attractive relocation package and support for a smooth relocation for you and your family
All applications will be treated with strict confidentiality!

 3+ years of experience in a similar role within the iGaming industry;
 Degree in Computer Science, Mathematics, Statistics or equivalent;
 Passionate about data and on the lookout for opportunities to optimise;
 Ability to comprehend business background and translate into measurable metrics;
 Meaningful communicator ‚Äî a storyteller who can deliver the right analytics for the target audience;

Skills Requirements

Project details

The Data & Analytics department owns the group‚Äôs data stack spanning Data Engineering, Business Intelligence and Analytics & Insights to enable the company to deliver exceptional customer experience and become more data driven.

Team Lead of Insights and Analytics
will be leading a team of analysts to leverage the data assets in this central function to establish and deliver analytics to help guide and support internal business units and external partners in their understanding of client behaviour.

------------------------Job requirements
Key responsibilities:
Develop and manage key revenue and marketing funnel metrics to drive revenue growth and enable forecasting
Create data-driven insights about the impact of our global performance marketing campaigns
Develop new approaches to grow our user base through data-driven marketing optimization
Build intuitive and readable dashboards using visualization tools (e.g., Tableau, GDS) and alerting systems for the ongoing analysis of marketing campaigns, tests, and channels
Maintain data in a central location, easily accessible, and provide training in how to use it
Own our data infrastructure, including the design and maintenance of ETLs for impact reporting, attribution
Influence backend data design and develop your own data solutions as needed
Partner with our data science team to create deep insights into our new user cohorts
Collaborate with different marketing functions to create analyses to help support campaign decisions
Proactively surface potential problems within the marketing funnel and work with Marketing/Sales leaders to create action plans
Build data models that can be used by marketing to understand the efficacy of their programs
Lead cross-functional workstreams with teams to unify and improve data availability to and from new tools and sources
Be the resident expert in experimental design including A/B testing, incrementality measurement, and attribution.
Convert complex data and findings into understandable tables, graphs, and written reports
Work with stakeholders to determine success metrics, forecast spending, and drive performance improvements
Skills and expertise:
2+ years of SQL experience and a high level of comfort in manipulating/joining data sets from different sources, extracting, cleaning, and transforming data in large, complex, nested, databases
2+ years experience in SaaS product marketing and data analytics
At least 2 years of relevant work experience as an analyst, data scientist, market researcher, or similar role involving analyzing datasets and developing actionable insights from them
Solid digital marketing background
Experience with different marketing attribution methodologies
Proficiency with data visualization tools such as Tableau or Data Studio for full-stack data analysis, insight synthesis, and presentation
Strong ability to condense complex concepts and analysis into clear and concise takeaways that drive action
The ability to connect data to outcomes (identify cause and effect). We want you to be able to tell us what the data says and what we should do next.
Relevant technical skills may include marketing automation tools, Hubspot, Google Analytics, Amplitude, GoogleDataStudio, SQL, Big Query, Tableau, or similar
Expert in Microsoft Excel and Proficient with Google Docs
Excellent communication and organizational skills

The Role:
We are looking for a Cloud Security Analyst, specifically experienced with AWS, to join our fast-growing team. The successful candidate will contribute to our operational security both in terms of detection and response. The team is responsible for end-to-end operational security and utilises cutting edge technology from reputable vendors such as SIEM, EDR and CASB among others.
The
main responsibilities of the position include:
Responsible for end-to-end operational security and incident response with focus on AWS
SIEM maintenance and monitoring, including other security tools
Develop and maintain incident response triage guides and playbooks
Provide incident response training to other teams and conduct tabletop exercises
Cooperate with other teams to improve the company security posture
Report and stay abreast of current security threats
Maintain security solutions such as next-generation firewalls, email security technologies, CASB, EDR and DLP
Main requirements:
BSc/MSc in information security, or any other related field
Minimum 2 years‚Äô working experience as a security analyst
Working experience with AWS cloud security and incident investigation
Solid understanding of incident response
Experience with playbook and SIEM correlation search development
Experience with threat hunting, red/blue teaming and threat intelligence
Good knowledge of security technologies such as firewalls, EDR, SIEM, CASB, WAF, AWS Inspector, CloudTrail and GuardDuty
Knowledge of various information system technologies (Windows/Linux systems, Active Directory, VMware, databases etc)
Excellent communication and documentation skills
Strong analytical and problem-solving abilities
Self-motivated with a keen attention to detail
Benefit from:
Attractive remuneration package
Food allowance
Intellectually stimulating work environment
Continuous personal development and international training opportunities
Attractive relocation package and support for a smooth relocation for you and your family
Type of employment: Full time
Location: Cyprus, Greece, Remote
Please visit our website
www.xm.com/careers
to submit your online application for this position.
All applications will be treated with strict confidentiality!

------------------------General requirements.
Business Intelligence Lead will work with internal and external clients to implement BI reporting projects. You will manage a team of BI developers, supervising them on all the stages of project implementation, incl. requirement gathering, development, testing, deployment, and user training and support.
Qualifications:
A degree in data analytics, computer science, economics, or finance.
3-5
years of experience in a data-related or business intelligence position.
Management / Supervisory experience
Knowledge of BI tools, concepts and architecture, and decision support concepts
Knowledge of ETL and data analysis with a focus on data integrity
Knowledge of BI Stack, including Azure BI Services, MSSQL, SSIS, SSAS, Power BI
Strong ability to share knowledge, coach, and train others
Experience translating business requirements into technical requirements that can be directly actioned by BI developers
Interpersonal skills suited to dealing courteously and professionally with cross-functional stakeholders.
Excellent presentation skills.
English from Upper-Intermediate.
Would be nice to have:
Experience with Dynamics 365
Experience in the construction industry
Years of experience.
5+ years of experience in Business Intelligence as a Consultant or Senior Consultant
BI Lead (Consultant/Senior Consultant) responsibilities:
Manage the BI development team in order to ensure effective BI tools are developed for the internal and external stakeholders
Work with Business Leadership to identify reporting needs, manage priorities and assess data readiness.
Define the business requirements and translate them into technical specifications
Define the scope of work and ensure timely execution of requirements to meet business needs.
Work with BI Developers to create analytics reports/dashboards that translate data and insights into visuals and narratives that are easy to understand, can impact decisions, and drive business goals.
Work with data sources and data flows to ensure accuracy, validity, and data integrity.
Perform user acceptance of delivered reports, confirming the accuracy of report and compliance to pre-defined requirements.
Identify future-state BI innovations including new data sources and tools to provide additional insights.
Support the deployment of new analytics by delivering appropriate training and preparing training materials.
Overseeing internal and external BI projects under your supervision from the beginning to the end.
Ensure the business is provided with operational support and technical issues for BI processes are solved effectively.
Conduct performance reviews and monthly one-on-one meetings with the BI development team
Set team objectives and monitor progress towards achieving them
Coach and mentor the BI developers
Manage own professional and self-development

Responsibilities
With Teiva Systems, our clients can optimize internal processes and save valuable time and money. The ServiceNow Consultant & Business Analyst will be working with our large enterprise clients on performing business value assessments (BVA) to visualize and quantify this optimization potential. This includes assessing and mapping out existing processes using BPMN and identifying pain points and understanding resource requirements. In a second step, the Business Analyst will compare the current state to potential solution scenarios leveraging. The Business Analyst will lead meetings with cross-functional teams of our worldwide customers and requires strong English communication and analytical skills. The Business Analyst will also ensure that customer input and feedback gathered during these BVAs are shared with project and product owners for continuous improvement of our solution.
You will:
‚Äî Work with our customers on analyzing processes.
‚Äî Map customer business processes and identify pain points and resource requirements.
‚Äî Compare current state and potential process scenarios.
‚Äî Generate business value analysis for our customers together with our sales team.
‚Äî Collaborate across teams to collect inputs and share feedback.
‚Äî Gathering requirements, find out clients‚Äô business needs.
‚Äî Writing project documentation.
‚Äî Producing business requirement artifacts.
‚Äî Hold training sessions for system end users.
Project description
Teiva Systems specialists have been developing on ServiceNow platform since 2007. We offer managed services to companies that own ServiceNow in Germany, Switzerland and Israel. We also specialize in developing business applications. We strive to help organizations maximize productivity, reduce risks, and accelerate time-to-value with the help of ITSM, ITAM, ITOM, ITBM, HR Management and IoT Devise Management.
Teiva Systems is looking for a Senior ServiceNow Consultant & Business Analyst with a high degree of readiness for active work and workload.

—î –æ–¥–Ω–∏–º —ñ–∑ –Ω–∞–π–±—ñ–ª—å—à–∏—Ö –≥–ª–æ–±–∞–ª—å–Ω–∏—Ö –ø–∞–±–ª—ñ—à–µ—Ä—ñ–≤ –Ω–µ—ñ–≥—Ä–æ–≤–∏—Ö –∑–∞—Å—Ç–æ—Å—É–Ω–∫—ñ–≤. –á—Ö –∑–∞–≤–∞–Ω—Ç–∞–∂–∏–ª–∏ –ø–æ–Ω–∞–¥ 300 –º—ñ–ª—å–π–æ–Ω—ñ–≤ —Ä–∞–∑—ñ–≤. –©–æ–º—ñ—Å—è—Ü—è –∑–∞—Å—Ç–æ—Å—É–Ω–∫–∞–º–∏ –∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É—é—Ç—å—Å—è –¥–µ—Å—è—Ç–∫–∏ –º—ñ–ª—å–π–æ–Ω—ñ–≤ –ª—é–¥–µ–π –∑ —É—Å—å–æ–≥–æ —Å–≤—ñ—Ç—É.
–í
Genesis
–Ω–∞—Ä–æ–¥–∏–ª–∏—Å—è —Ç–∞ —Å—Ç–∞–ª–∏ —Å–∞–º–æ—Å—Ç—ñ–π–Ω–∏–º–∏ –±—ñ–∑–Ω–µ—Å–∞–º–∏ —É—Å–ø—ñ—à–Ω—ñ –∫–æ–º–ø–∞–Ω—ñ—ó: –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥, Jiji, BetterMe, Headway. –í –µ–∫–æ—Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ñ —Ç–∞–∫–æ–∂ —Ä–æ–∑–≤–∏–≤–∞—é—Ç—å—Å—è –ø—Ä–æ—î–∫—Ç–∏ OBRIO, Boosters, AMO, Universe.

Sendios
–ø—Ä–∞—Ü—é—î –∑ –º–∞–ª–∏–º–∏ —Ç–∞ –≤–µ–ª–∏–∫–∏–º–∏ –∫–æ–º–ø–∞–Ω—ñ—è–º–∏ —Ç–∞ –¥–æ–ø–æ–º–∞–≥–∞—î —ó–º –¥–æ—Å—è–≥—Ç–∏ –±—ñ–∑–Ω–µ—Å-—Ü—ñ–ª–µ–π –∑–∞ –¥–æ–ø–æ–º–æ–≥–æ—é –µ–ª–µ–∫—Ç—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –º–∞—Ä–∫–µ—Ç–∏–Ω–≥—É. –ù–∞—à–∞ –ø–ª–∞—Ç—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞ —Ç–∞ –¥–æ—Å–≤—ñ–¥ –¥–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—é—Ç—å –Ω–∞–º –∑–º—ñ—Ü–Ω—é–≤–∞—Ç–∏ –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥—É –∫–ª—ñ—î–Ω—Ç–∞, –æ—Å–∫—ñ–ª—å–∫–∏ –º–∏ —Å–∞–º—ñ –ø—ñ–∫–ª—É—î–º–æ—Å—è –ø—Ä–æ –≤–µ—Å—å –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å. –ú–∏ –ø–æ—Å—Ç—ñ–π–Ω–æ –≤–¥–æ—Å–∫–æ–Ω–∞–ª—é—î–º–æ –Ω–∞—à—ñ –ø–æ—Å–ª—É–≥–∏, —â–æ–± –∑—Ä–æ–±–∏—Ç–∏ –∑–Ω–∞—á–Ω–∏–π –≤–Ω–µ—Å–æ–∫ —É –∑—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–Ω—è –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑–Ω–∏–∫—ñ–≤ –ø—Ä–æ–¥—É–∫—Ç—ñ–≤ –Ω–∞—à–∏—Ö –∫–ª—ñ—î–Ω—Ç—ñ–≤ —ñ —Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—è —ñ–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü—ñ–π–Ω–∏—Ö email-—Ä–æ–∑—Å–∏–ª–æ–∫.
–Ø–∫ Product Analyst —É Sendios
, —Ç–∏ –¥–æ–ø–æ–º–æ–∂–µ—à –Ω–∞—à—ñ–π –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥—ñ –ø—Ä–∏–π–º–∞—Ç–∏ –∫—Ä–∞—â—ñ —Ä—ñ—à–µ–Ω–Ω—è, –≤—ñ–¥—Å—Ç–æ—é—é—á–∏ –ø—ñ–¥—Ö–æ–¥–∏ –Ω–∞ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤—ñ –¥–∞–Ω–∏—Ö —É –≤—Å—ñ–π –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥—ñ. –¢–≤—ñ–π –∞–Ω–∞–ª—ñ–∑ —Å–ø—Ä–∏—è—Ç–∏–º–µ –Ω–∞—à—ñ–π —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥—ñ—ó –≤ —Ç–∞–∫–∏—Ö —Å—Ñ–µ—Ä–∞—Ö, —è–∫ –∑–∞–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–≤–∞—á—ñ–≤, –∑–∞–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è, —É—Ç—Ä–∏–º–∞–Ω–Ω—è —Ç–æ—â–æ. –ú–∏ –Ω–∞–π–º–∞—î–º–æ –ª—é–¥–µ–π, —è–∫–∏–º –¥–æ–≤—ñ—Ä—è—î–º–æ, —ñ –Ω–∞–¥–∞—î–º–æ —á–ª–µ–Ω–∞–º –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥–∏ –∞–≤—Ç–æ–Ω–æ–º—ñ—é, —â–æ–± –≤–æ–Ω–∏ —è–∫–Ω–∞–π–∫—Ä–∞—â–µ –ø—Ä–∞—Ü—é–≤–∞–ª–∏, –ø—Ä–∏–π–º–∞–ª–∏ —Ä—ñ—à–µ–Ω–Ω—è —Ç–∞ –±—Ä–∞–ª–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∏—Ö –≤—ñ–¥–ø–æ–≤—ñ–¥–∞–ª—å–Ω—ñ—Å—Ç—å.
Sendios
—à—É–∫–∞—î –≤–º–æ—Ç–∏–≤–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ–≥–æ –µ–Ω—Ç—É–∑—ñ–∞—Å—Ç–∞, —è–∫–∏–π –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∏–π —É–≤—ñ–π—Ç–∏ –≤ –¥–∏–Ω–∞–º—ñ—á–Ω–µ —Å–µ—Ä–µ–¥–æ–≤–∏—â–µ, —â–æ —à–≤–∏–¥–∫–æ —Ä–æ–∑–≤–∏–≤–∞—î—Ç—å—Å—è, —ñ —è–∫—ñ—Å–Ω–æ –≤–ø–ª–∏–Ω—É—Ç–∏ –Ω–∞ –Ω—å–æ–≥–æ.

2+ —Ä–æ–∫–∏ –¥–æ—Å–≤—ñ–¥—É —Ä–æ–±–æ—Ç–∏ –∞–Ω–∞–ª—ñ—Ç–∏–∫–æ–º —É Product Team;

------------------------As a Business Analyst you act as a liaison between IT and business units for the development, implementation and support of new systems and enhancement under minimal guidance. You actively support and facilitate the gathering of our business needs and objectives to evaluate new or enhanced functionality.
In this role you document and test system requirements to solve complex problems and develop innovative solutions, working collaboratively with the development team and product owners.
‚Ä¢	Experience in business analysis, business rules and process analysis, creation of use cases and test cases for 3+ years.
‚Ä¢	Solid knowledge in preparation of requirement specifications on technical and business levels.
‚Ä¢	Strong communication skills, including high level of interpersonal and presentation skills
‚Ä¢	Flexible personality with strong analytical and problem-solving skills with the ability to thrive in a fast-paced environment
‚Ä¢	Self-motivated, detail-oriented and organized
‚Ä¢	Ability to write in a clear and concise manner and to communicate effectively in English
------------------------We are looking for a BA who has:
2+ years of experience as a Business/System Analyst;
Analytical and communications skills necessary to elicit and define business requirements and translate them into solutions;
Strong system analysis skills (data modeling);
Understanding of REST API;

Basic knowledge of SQL and understanding of how relational data bases work, ability to read the DB schema;
Can speak and write in English at an
upper-intermediate or higher level
and efficiently communicate ideas, design, and document artifacts concisely.
Manifests KindGeek corporate values ‚Äî trust, transparency, social responsibility, and the sense of beauty.
As a BA You will:
Defining and prioritizing high-level requirements;
Collecting estimates from developers;
Preparing roadmaps;
Specifying low-level requirements based on spoken and written communication with the technical customer;
Reviewing visual prototypes;
Preparing scope of the sprint ‚Äî creating user stories, conducting groomings and plannings with the team;
Functional testing of the self-prepared part of the scope;
Analyzing 3rd parties API documentation and creating integration requirements for back-end developers.
About the project
The client is one of the most famous Swiss universities, traditionally featuring in various TOP-100 world universities rankings. Being an innovative institution, the university has gone through a digital transformation in recent years. We are working on the solution that combines features of the Research Information System and Campus Management Platform.
As a Research Information System, the solution allows to track the academic progress of the research fellows within the university. The system automatically generates personal reports for researchers based on a list of KPIs, such as number of the academic publications within a certain timeframe and department, number of the research grants obtained and amount of funds raised for each etc. Reports can be used for personal reasons as well as to make decisions about the academic promotion of the university staff. The Research Information System is currently used within the medical faculty, however, the expansion to other faculties is expected in the near future. As a Campus Management System, the solution can be useful in several ways: to generate professors‚Äô and students‚Äô personal schedules, assign rooms and track professors‚Äô workload.
The project offers complex business challenges from the perspective of business logic and opportunities for growth and personal development.

—Å–ø—ñ–≤–ø—Ä–∞—Ü—é–≤–∞—Ç–∏ –∑ –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥–æ—é –∫–ª—ñ—î–Ω—Ç—ñ–≤, —â–æ–± –Ω–∞–¥–∞—Ç–∏ —ó–º —É—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø—Ä–æ –º–æ–∂–ª–∏–≤–æ—Å—Ç—ñ –∑—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–Ω—è, —è–∫—ñ –≤–∏–Ω–∏–∫–∞—é—Ç—å –Ω–∞ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤—ñ –Ω–∞—à–∏—Ö –¥–∞–Ω–∏—Ö;

—Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ä—é–≤–∞—Ç–∏ —Å–ø–µ—Ü—ñ–∞–ª—å–Ω—ñ –∑–≤—ñ—Ç–∏;
–ø—Ä–æ–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç–∏ –¥–æ—Å–ª—ñ–¥–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—è –Ω–æ–≤–∏—Ö –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑–Ω–∏–∫—ñ–≤.
Hard skills:
2+ —Ä–æ–∫–∏ –¥–æ—Å–≤—ñ–¥—É —Ä–æ–±–æ—Ç–∏ –∞–Ω–∞–ª—ñ—Ç–∏–∫–æ–º —É Product Team;

–≤—ñ–ª—å–Ω–µ –≤–æ–ª–æ–¥—ñ–Ω–Ω—è —ñ–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞–º–∏ BI/–≤—ñ–∑—É–∞–ª—ñ–∑–∞—Ü—ñ—ó –¥–ª—è –∑–≤—ñ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—ñ (Tableau);

–∑–¥–∞—Ç–Ω—ñ—Å—Ç—å –ø—Ä–∞—Ü—é–≤–∞—Ç–∏ —Å–∞–º–æ—Å—Ç—ñ–π–Ω–æ —Ç–∞ —Å–ø—ñ–ª—å–Ω–æ –≤ –¥–∏–Ω–∞–º—ñ—á–Ω–æ–º—É —Å–µ—Ä–µ–¥–æ–≤–∏—â—ñ;
–∫—Ä–µ–∞—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–µ –º–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—è, –º–æ—Ç–∏–≤–∞—Ü—ñ—è –¥–æ –≤–∏–∫–ª–∏–∫—ñ–≤ —ñ –ø–æ—Å—Ç—ñ–π–Ω–µ –ø—Ä–∞–≥–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω—è –¥–æ –∫—Ä–∞—â–æ–≥–æ;

–©–æ –º–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–ø–æ–Ω—É—î–º–æ:
–∫–æ–º—Ñ–æ—Ä—Ç–Ω—ñ —É–º–æ–≤–∏
: –∑–∞—Ç–∏—à–Ω–∏–π –æ—Ñ—ñ—Å (5 —Ö–≤ –ø—ñ—à–∫–∏ –¥–æ –º–µ—Ç—Ä–æ –¢–∞—Ä–∞—Å–∞ –®–µ–≤—á–µ–Ω–∫–∞) –∑ —Ç–µ—Ä–∞—Å–æ—é, –ª–∞—É–Ω–∂ –∑–æ–Ω–∞–º–∏, –∫—É—Ö–Ω–µ—é, –∫–∞–≤‚Äô—è—Ä–Ω–µ—é. –°–ø–µ—Ü—ñ–∞–ª—å–Ω–∞ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞ –≤–µ–Ω—Ç–∏–ª—è—Ü—ñ—ó, –∫–æ–Ω–¥–∏—Ü—ñ–æ–Ω—É–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—è, –æ—á–∏—â–µ–Ω–Ω—è —Ç–∞ –∑–≤–æ–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–æ–≤—ñ—Ç—Ä—è. –¢—Ä–∞–Ω—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç, —â–æ–± –¥—ñ–±—Ä–∞—Ç–∏—Å—è –¥–æ –æ—Ñ—ñ—Å—É –∞–±–æ –æ–±–ª–∞–¥–Ω–∞–Ω–Ω—è –¥–æ–º–∞—à–Ω—å–æ–≥–æ –æ—Ñ—ñ—Å—É –ø—ñ–¥ —á–∞—Å –∫–∞—Ä–∞–Ω—Ç–∏–Ω—É;
—Ç—É—Ä–±–æ—Ç–∞ –ø—Ä–æ –∑–¥–æ—Ä–æ–≤‚Äô—è
: —Å–Ω—ñ–¥–∞–Ω–∫–∏, –≤–µ—á–µ—Ä—ñ, –Ω–µ–æ–±–º–µ–∂–µ–Ω–∞ –∫—ñ–ª—å–∫—ñ—Å—Ç—å —Ñ—Ä—É–∫—Ç—ñ–≤, —Å–æ–∫—ñ–≤, –ø–µ—Ä–µ–∫—É—Å—ñ–≤. –ö–æ—Ä–ø–æ—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–∏–π –ª—ñ–∫–∞—Ä —ñ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ö—É–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—è. –í—ñ–¥—à–∫–æ–¥—É–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—è –≤–∏—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç –Ω–∞ —Ç–µ—Å—Ç—É–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—è —Ç–∞ –ª—ñ–∫—É–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—è COVID-19 –¥–ª—è –ø—Ä–∞—Ü—ñ–≤–Ω–∏–∫—ñ–≤ —Ç–∞ —ó—Ö–Ω—ñ—Ö —Ä–æ–¥–∏–Ω. –ë–µ–∑–∫–æ—à—Ç–æ–≤–Ω—ñ —Ç—Ä–µ–Ω—É–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—è –∑ –±—ñ–≥—É, —Ñ—É—Ç–±–æ–ª—É, –±–∞—Å–∫–µ—Ç–±–æ–ª—É, –≤–æ–ª–µ–π–±–æ–ª—É, –π–æ–≥–∏. –ó–Ω–∏–∂–∫–∏ –≤ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–µ–≥–ª–∏—Ö —Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∑–∞–ª–∞—Ö —ñ –æ–ø–ª–∞—Ç–∞ —É—á–∞—Å—Ç—ñ –≤ —Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–∏—Ö –∑–º–∞–≥–∞–Ω–Ω—è—Ö;

–ù–µ –∑–≤–æ–ª—ñ–∫–∞–π —ñ —Å–∫–æ—Ä—ñ—à–µ –ø–æ–¥–∞–≤–∞–π —Å–≤–æ—î —Ä–µ–∑—é–º–µ!
------------------------–ù–µ–æ–±—Ö—ñ–¥–Ω—ñ –Ω–∞–≤–∏—á–∫–∏
üîπ–°–∏–ª—å–Ω—ñ –Ω–∞–≤–∏—á–∫–∏ –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏—á–Ω–æ–≥–æ –º–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—è
üîπ–ì–∞—Ä–Ω—ñ –∫–æ–º—É–Ω—ñ–∫–∞—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ñ –Ω–∞–≤–∏—á–∫–∏

üîπ–ê–Ω–≥–ª—ñ–π—Å—å–∫–∞ –º–æ–≤–∞ Upper-Intermediate+ (—É—Å–Ω–∞ —Ç–∞ –ø–∏—Å—å–º–æ–≤–∞)
–û—Å–æ–±–∏—Å—Ç—ñ —è–∫–æ—Å—Ç—ñ:

üîπ–£ –≤–∞—Å –≤–∏—Å–æ–∫–∞ –µ–º–ø–∞—Ç—ñ—è —Ç–∞ –≥–ª–∏–±–æ–∫–µ —Ä–æ–∑—É–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–æ—Ç—Ä–µ–± –ª—é–¥–µ–π –Ω–∞–≤–∫–æ–ª–æ –≤–∞—Å

–ë—É–¥–µ –ø–ª—é—Å–æ–º:

------------------------We are looking for a Design Business Analyst/UX Architect to join our inhouse design team. You will manage the client‚Äôs expectations while overseeing the solution‚Äôs progress and the interface designers‚Äô team. We are pursuing the following industries (but not limited to): Professional Services, including Financial and Accounting web and mobile applications; Digital Services: Human Resources, Remote work, Productivity related systems; Ecommerce; Logistics and Transportation, and more.
Requirements
General:
You worked with creative teams and clients before (agency or studio experience will a huge plus)
You know how to gather requirements in the way the team expects it ‚Äî it is better to work with creative briefs rather than with ready-made solutions
You hear the customer, but you do not let them manage your team
Practical:
Design creation and project flow understanding ‚Äî it is important to us that you know how an interface is created and implemented
Design background and understanding of the UX principles is a HUGE plus
Can suggest design solutions when the designer is not available (e.g. on the client call)
Strong knowledge of PM methodologies (Agile and Waterfall) including project planning, goal setting, risk and time management, evaluation and allocation of the resources and more
Knowledge of theoretical and practical aspects of SAFe
Experience in task & time tracking systems (we use ClickUp)
Experience in board collaboration and mind mapping tools (we mostly use Miro and FigJam)
Basic knowledge of Figma functionality (we expect that you will be able to navigate, copy and move mockup elements, change UX copy)
Knowledge of design process methodologies (Agile UX and Lean UX)
You can work with the data in the spreadsheets (Excel or Google Spreadsheets), you can easily organize it and use formulas to speed up the process
Understanding of UX Writing principles will be a plus
Understanding of WCAG principles will be a plus
Basic knowledge of HCD, UCD and other methodologies will be a plus
Knowledge of web analytics tools (Google or Adobe Omniture) & data visualization tools (Power BI or Tableau) will be a plus
Knowledge of SDLS will be a plus
Soft:
Strong organisational and analytical skills with high attention to details
We work better with goal-oriented person that can adjust the project processes to the actual client needs
We would love to share the same mindset with you ‚Äî provide the best solution to the client based on the team expertise & business and user needs
Be ready to share and follow the team‚Äôs values and principles
Ability to independently maintain tasks, make informed decisions and take responsibility for them
It is important for you to properly communicate and interact with people including making and receiving productive feedback
You are passionate to learn and try new ideas
Be flexible and adaptive to a situatevely fast paced environment
Be proactive, positive and upbeat, with a sense of ownership
Written project cases from your previous experience will be a plus.
Languages:
English: all of our clients speak English, so it is crucial for you to have at least Upper-Intermediate+ / B2+ level (IELTS or TOEFL certification will be a plus)
Responsibilities:
Manage a design team on a project
Leading the client (keeping in mind that the project ownership is on your side)
Gathering requirements
Validation of the project scope with the team and confirmation of it with the client
Create and manage feasible timelines
Maintain a project backlog
Timely response to customer requests & clearly address them to the design team
Risk management
Perform and manage design demos
Create and maintain project documentation
Create and maintain tasks within the task-tracking toolset
Communicate and establish a delivery process with the development team
What we offer:
Team of talented and appreciative open-minded professionals
Regular feedback and health checks
Medical insurance and sports program compensation
Paid English language courses
Private Entrepreneur and legal support
We currently work from home with office essentials and support, but you can visit our office in Kyiv if you wish so
Shifted working hours (11am‚Äî8pm)
About us
We are Trinetix ‚Äî a dynamic, rapidly growing technology organization with approximately 700 representatives in Europe, the United States, and Ukraine, who bring their passion, skill & innovation to ensure our organization provides products that meet the needs of our partners and clients.
We offer IT solutions to business enterprises of various sizes and industries using the latest cutting-edge technologies. We assist our clients and partners in improving work processes, making them more efficient, and keeping the essential objectives focused. We serve and support various business entities, enterprises, and startups globally, to grow and stay competitive in the digital era. We achieve this important goal by efficiently implementing tech innovation, substantial professional expertise, and a solution-driven strategy.

‚Äî transformers devoted to the country. There are about 60 of us. We have created a two-level system of auctions for the sale, lease or distribution of state and communal assets. We are one of the few companies in Ukraine that is both a state-owned enterprise, an IT startup and the driving force behind a whole series of reforms.
Even before the war, our reforms enriched the state budget and local budgets of various levels by more than 62 billion hryvnias. And now we are making even more efforts to support, restore and develop the economic system of our Ukraine. In our free time, we volunteer and help the Armed Forces.
During the war, with the help of our system, the organizers earned more than 1 billion hryvnias for the budgets of various levels. We have created charity auctions to support the army and humanitarian needs. And we have many more qualitatively new projects in the plans.

‚Äî Identification, analysis and determination of requirements for the launch of new auction procedures and the development of existing ones (from the sale of assets of bankrupt banks and privatization to the lease of state and communal property in Ukraine and mining rights);

AUTOMAT-IT is a DevOps company that was founded in 2012 (Tel Aviv, Israel).
We are a growing provider of DevOps and Cloud Professional Services. We help our customers manage DevOps and Cloud environments from initial design through build, deployment, and ongoing management. We run various projects from startups to enterprises, both short and long-term.
We are architects, engineers, developers, and project managers who recognize the importance and opportunity of creating integrated, cross-functional dev and ops teams to maximize productivity.
